[←4. Quantifiers and Equality](Quantifiers-and-Equality/#quantifiers-and-equality "4. Quantifiers and Equality")[6. Interacting with Lean→](Interacting-with-Lean/#Theorem-Proving-in-Lean-4--Interacting-with-Lean "6. Interacting with Lean")
#  5. Tactics
In this chapter, we describe an alternative approach to constructing proofs, using _tactics_. A proof term is a representation of a mathematical proof; tactics are commands, or instructions, that describe how to build such a proof. Informally, you might begin a mathematical proof by saying “to prove the forward direction, unfold the definition, apply the previous lemma, and simplify.” Just as these are instructions that tell the reader how to find the relevant proof, tactics are instructions that tell Lean how to construct a proof term. They naturally support an incremental style of writing proofs, in which you decompose a proof and work on goals one step at a time.
We will describe proofs that consist of sequences of tactics as “tactic-style” proofs, to contrast with the ways of writing proof terms we have seen so far, which we will call “term-style” proofs. Each style has its own advantages and disadvantages. For example, tactic-style proofs can be harder to read, because they require the reader to predict or guess the results of each instruction. But they can also be shorter and easier to write. Moreover, tactics offer a gateway to using Lean's automation, since automated procedures are themselves tactics.
##  5.1. Entering Tactic Mode[🔗](find/?domain=Verso.Genre.Manual.section&name=entering-tactic-mode "Permalink")
Conceptually, stating a theorem or introducing a `have` statement creates a goal, namely, the goal of constructing a term with the expected type. For example, the following creates the goal of constructing a term of type `p ∧ q ∧ p`, in a context with constants `p q : Prop`, `hp : p` and `hq : q`:
`theorem `declaration uses 'sorry'`test (p q : Prop) (hp : p) (hq : q) : p ∧ q ∧ p := byp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p [sorry](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#sorry "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")All goals completed! 🐙 ```
You can write this goal as follows:
p:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p
Indeed, if you replace the “sorry” by an underscore in the example above, Lean will report that it is exactly this goal that has been left unsolved.
Ordinarily, you meet such a goal by writing an explicit term. But wherever a term is expected, Lean allows us to insert instead a `by <tactics>` block, where `<tactics>` is a sequence of commands, separated by semicolons or line breaks. You can prove the theorem above in that way:
`theorem test (p q : Prop) (hp : p) (hq : q) : p ∧ q ∧ p :=   byp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [And.intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")leftp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ prightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p      [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hprightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p      [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [And.intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")right.leftp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ qright.rightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p      [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hqright.rightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p      [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hpAll goals completed! 🐙 ```
We often put the `by` keyword on the preceding line, and write the example above as:
`theorem test (p q : Prop) (hp : p) (hq : q) : p ∧ q ∧ p := byp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p   [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [And.intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")leftp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ prightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p   [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hprightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p   [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [And.intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")right.leftp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ qright.rightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p   [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hqright.rightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p   [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hpAll goals completed! 🐙 ```
The `[apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` tactic applies an expression, viewed as denoting a function with zero or more arguments. It unifies the conclusion with the expression in the current goal, and creates new goals for the remaining arguments, provided that no later arguments depend on them. In the example above, the command `[apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [And.intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")` yields two subgoals:
leftp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ prightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p
The first goal is met with the command `[exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hp`. The `[exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` command is just a variant of `[apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` which signals that the expression given should fill the goal exactly. It is good form to use it in a tactic proof, since its failure signals that something has gone wrong. It is also more robust than `[apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")`, since the elaborator takes the expected type, given by the target of the goal, into account when processing the expression that is being applied. In this case, however, `[apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` would work just as well.
You can see the resulting proof term with the `#print` command:
`theorem test (p q : Prop) (hp : p) (hq : q) : p ∧ q ∧ p := byp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p   [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [And.intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")leftp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ prightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p   [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hprightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p   [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [And.intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")right.leftp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ qright.rightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p   [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hqright.rightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p   [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hpAll goals completed! 🐙 `
``theorem test : ∀ (p q : Prop), p → q → p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p := fun p q hp hq => [⟨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")hp[,](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference") [⟨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")hq[,](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference") hp[⟩](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")[⟩](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")`#print test`
```
theorem test : ∀ (p q : Prop), p → q → p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p :=
fun p q hp hq => [⟨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")hp[,](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference") [⟨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")hq[,](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference") hp[⟩](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")[⟩](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")
```
``
You can write a tactic script incrementally. In VS Code, you can open a window to display messages by pressing ``Ctrl``Shift``Enter``, and that window will then show you the current goal whenever the cursor is in a tactic block. If the proof is incomplete, the token `by` is decorated with a red squiggly line, and the error message contains the remaining goals.
Tactic commands can take compound expressions, not just single identifiers. The following is a shorter version of the preceding proof:
`theorem test (p q : Prop) (hp : p) (hq : q) : p ∧ q ∧ p := byp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p   [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [And.intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference") hpp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p   [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [And.intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference") hq hpAll goals completed! 🐙 ```
Unsurprisingly, it produces exactly the same proof term:
`theorem test (p q : Prop) (hp : p) (hq : q) : p ∧ q ∧ p := byp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p  [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [And.intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference") hpp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p  [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [And.intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference") hq hpAll goals completed! 🐙 `
``theorem test : ∀ (p q : Prop), p → q → p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p := fun p q hp hq => [⟨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")hp[,](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference") [⟨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")hq[,](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference") hp[⟩](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")[⟩](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")`#print test`
```
theorem test : ∀ (p q : Prop), p → q → p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p :=
fun p q hp hq => [⟨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")hp[,](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference") [⟨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")hq[,](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference") hp[⟩](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")[⟩](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")
```
``
Multiple tactic applications can be written in a single line by concatenating with a semicolon.
`theorem test (p q : Prop) (hp : p) (hq : q) : p ∧ q ∧ p := byp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p   [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [And.intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference") hpp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p; [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [And.intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference") hq hpAll goals completed! 🐙 ```
Tactics that may produce multiple subgoals often tag them. For example, the tactic `[apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [And.intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")` tagged the first subgoal as `leftleftp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p`, and the second as `rightrightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p`. In the case of the `[apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` tactic, the tags are inferred from the parameters' names used in the `[And.intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")` declaration. You can structure your tactics using the notation `case`` <tag> => <tactics>`. The following is a structured version of our first tactic proof in this chapter.
`theorem test (p q : Prop) (hp : p) (hq : q) : p ∧ q ∧ p := byp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p   [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [And.intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")leftp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ prightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p   [case](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#case "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") left =>p:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hpAll goals completed! 🐙   [case](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#case "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") right =>p:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p     [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [And.intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")leftp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ qrightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p     [case](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#case "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") left =>p:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ q [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hqAll goals completed! 🐙     [case](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#case "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") right =>p:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hpAll goals completed! 🐙 ```
You can solve the subgoal `rightrightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p` before `leftleftp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p` using the `[case](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#case "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` notation:
`theorem test (p q : Prop) (hp : p) (hq : q) : p ∧ q ∧ p := byp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p   [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [And.intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")leftp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ prightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p   [case](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#case "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") right =>p:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p     [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [And.intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")leftp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ qrightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p     [case](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#case "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") left =>p:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ q [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hqAll goals completed! 🐙     [case](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#case "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") right =>p:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hpAll goals completed! 🐙   [case](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#case "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") left =>p:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hpAll goals completed! 🐙 ```
Note that Lean hides the other goals inside the `[case](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#case "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` block. After `[case](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#case "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") left =>`, the proof state is:
p:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ q
We say that `[case](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#case "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` is “focusing” on the selected goal. Moreover, Lean flags an error if the selected goal is not fully solved at the end of the `[case](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#case "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` block.
For simple subgoals, it may not be worth selecting a subgoal using its tag, but you may still want to structure the proof. Lean also provides the “bullet” notation `. <tactics>` (or `· <tactics>`) for structuring proofs:
`theorem test (p q : Prop) (hp : p) (hq : q) : p ∧ q ∧ p := byp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p   [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [And.intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")leftp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ prightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p   .leftp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hpAll goals completed! 🐙   .rightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [And.intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")right.leftp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ qright.rightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p     .right.leftp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ q [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hqAll goals completed! 🐙     .right.rightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hpAll goals completed! 🐙 ```
##  5.2. Basic Tactics[🔗](find/?domain=Verso.Genre.Manual.section&name=basic-tactics "Permalink")
In addition to `[apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` and `[exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")`, another useful tactic is `[intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")`, which introduces a hypothesis. What follows is an example of an identity from propositional logic that we proved in a previous chapter, now proved using tactics.
`example (p q r : Prop) : p ∧ (q ∨ r) ↔ (p ∧ q) ∨ (p ∧ r) := byp:Propq:Propr:Prop⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation The `[intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` command can more generally be used to introduce a variable of any type:
`example (α : Type) : α → α := byα:Type⊢ α → α   [intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") aα:Typea:α⊢ α   [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") aAll goals completed! 🐙  ``example (α : Type) : ∀ x : α, x = x := byα:Type⊢ ∀ (x : α), x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") x   [intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") xα:Typex:α⊢ x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") x   [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [Eq.refl](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq.refl in Lean Language Reference") xAll goals completed! 🐙 ```
You can use it to introduce several variables:
`example : ∀ a b c : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference"), a = b → a = c → c = b := by⊢ ∀ (a b c As the `[apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` tactic is a command for constructing function applications interactively, the `[intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` tactic is a command for constructing function abstractions interactively (i.e., terms of the form `fun x => e`). As with lambda abstraction notation, the `[intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` tactic allows us to use an implicit `match`.
`example (p q : α → Prop) : (∃ x, p x ∧ q x) → ∃ x, q x ∧ p x := byα:Sort u_1p:α → Propq:α → Prop⊢ [(](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference")[∃](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") x[,](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") p x [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q x[)](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") → [∃](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") x[,](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") q x [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p x   [intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") ⟨w, hpw, hqw⟩α:Sort u_1p:α → Propq:α → Propw:αhpw:p whqw:q w⊢ [∃](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") x[,](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") q x [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p x   [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") ⟨w, hqw, hpw⟩All goals completed! 🐙 ```
You can also provide multiple alternatives like in the `match` expression.
`example (p q : α → Prop) : (∃ x, p x ∨ q x) → ∃ x, q x ∨ p x := byα:Sort u_1p:α → Propq:α → Prop⊢ [(](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro The `[intros](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intros "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` tactic can be used without any arguments, in which case, it chooses names and introduces as many variables as it can. You will see an example of this in a moment.
The `[assumption](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#assumption "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` tactic looks through the assumptions in context of the current goal, and if there is one matching the conclusion, it applies it.
`[variable](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Namespaces-and-Sections/#Lean___Parser___Command___variable "Documentation for syntax in Lean Language Reference") (x y z w : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference"))  ``example (h₁ : x = y) (h₂ : y = z) (h₃ : z = w) : x = w := byx:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")y:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")z:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")w:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")h₁:x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") yh₂:y [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") zh₃:z [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") w⊢ x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") w   [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [Eq.trans](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___trans "Documentation for Eq.trans in Lean Language Reference") h₁x:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") zh₃:z [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") w⊢ y [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") w [Eq.trans](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___trans "Documentation for Eq.trans in Lean Language Reference") h₂x:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language It will unify metavariables in the conclusion if necessary:
`[variable](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Namespaces-and-Sections/#Lean___Parser___Command___variable "Documentation for syntax in Lean Language Reference") (x y z w : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference"))  ``example (h₁ : x = y) (h₂ : y = z) (h₃ : z = w) : x = w := byx:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")y:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")z:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")w:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")h₁:x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") yh₂:y [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") zh₃:z [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") w⊢ x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") w The following example uses the `[intros](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intros "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` command to introduce the three variables and two hypotheses automatically:

Note that names automatically generated by Lean are inaccessible by default. The motivation is to ensure your tactic proofs do not rely on automatically generated names, and are consequently more robust. However, you can use the combinator `[unhygienic](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#unhygienic "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` to disable this restriction.
`example : ∀ a b c : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference"), a = b → a = c → c = b := by⊢ ∀ (a b c : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")), a [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") b → a [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") c → c [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") b [unhygienic](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#unhygienic "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")   [intros](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intros "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")a:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")b:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")c:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")a_1:a [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") ba_2:a [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") c⊢ c [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") b   [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [Eq.trans](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___trans "Documentation for Eq.trans in Lean Language Reference")h₁a:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")b:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")c:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")a_1:a You can also use the `[rename_i](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#rename_i "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` tactic to rename the most recent inaccessible names in your context. In the following example, the tactic `[rename_i](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#rename_i "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") h1 _ h2` renames two of the last three hypotheses in your context.
`example : ∀ a b c d : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference"), a = b → a = d → a = c → c = b := by⊢ ∀ (a b c d : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")), a [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") b → a [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") d → a [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") c → c The `[rfl](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#rfl "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` tactic solves goals that are reflexive relations applied to definitionally equal arguments. Equality is reflexive:
`example (y : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")) : (fun `unused variable `x`  Note: This linter can be disabled with `set_option linter.unusedVariables false``x : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") => 0) y = 0 := byy:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")⊢ (fun x => 0) y [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") 0 [rfl](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#rfl "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")All goals completed! 🐙 ```
The `[repeat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#repeat "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` combinator can be used to apply a tactic several times:
`example : ∀ a b c : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference"), a = b → a = c → c = b := by⊢ ∀ (a b c : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")), a [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") b → a [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") c → c [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") b   [intros](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intros "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")a✝²:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")b✝:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")c✝:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")a✝¹:a✝² [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") b✝a✝:a✝² [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") c✝⊢ c✝ [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") b✝   [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [Eq.trans](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___trans "Documentation for Eq.trans in Lean Language Reference")h₁a✝²:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")b✝:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")c✝:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")a✝¹:a✝² [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") b✝a✝:a✝² [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") c✝⊢ c✝ [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") ?bh₂a✝²:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")b✝:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") b✝ba✝²:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")b✝:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")c✝:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")a✝¹:a✝² [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") b✝a✝:a✝² [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") c✝⊢ [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")   [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") Reference")h₁.ha✝²:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")c✝:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")a✝¹:a✝² [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") c✝h₂a✝²:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")b✝:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")c✝:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")a✝¹:a✝²
