[=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") b✝ba✝²:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")b✝:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")c✝:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")a✝¹:a✝² [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") b✝a✝:a✝² [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") c✝⊢ [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")   [repeat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#repeat "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [assumption](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#assumption "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")All goals completed! 🐙 ```
Another tactic that is sometimes useful is the `[revert](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#revert "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` tactic, which is, in a sense, an inverse to `[intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")`:
`example (x : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")) : x = x := byx:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")⊢ x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") x   [revert](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#revert "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") x⊢ ∀ (x : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")), x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") x   [intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") yy:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")⊢ y [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") y   [rfl](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#rfl "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")All goals completed! 🐙 ```
After `[revert](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#revert "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") x`, the proof state is:
⊢ ∀ (x : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")), x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") x
After `[intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") y`, it is:
y:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")⊢ y [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") y
Moving a hypothesis into the goal yields an implication:
`example (x y : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")) (h : x = y) : y = x := byx:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")y:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")h:x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") y⊢ y [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") x   [revert](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#revert "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hx:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")y:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")⊢ x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") y → y [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") x   [intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") h₁x:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")y:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")h₁:x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") y⊢ y [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") x   -- goal is x y : Nat, h₁ : x = y ⊢ y = x   [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [Eq.symm](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___symm "Documentation for Eq.symm in Lean Language Reference")hx:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")y:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")h₁:x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") y⊢ x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") y   [assumption](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#assumption "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")All goals completed! 🐙 ```
After `[revert](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#revert "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") h`, the proof state is:
x:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")y:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")⊢ x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") y → y [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") x
After `[intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") h₁`, it is:
x:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")y:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")h₁:x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") y⊢ y [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") x
But `[revert](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#revert "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` is even more clever, in that it will revert not only an element of the context but also all the subsequent elements of the context that depend on it. For example, reverting `x` in the example above brings `h` along with it:
`example (x y : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")) (h : x = y) : y = x := byx:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")y:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")h:x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") y⊢ y [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") x   [revert](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#revert "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") xy:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")⊢ ∀ (x : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")), x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") y → y [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") x   [intros](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intros "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")y:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")x✝:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")h✝:x✝ [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") y⊢ y [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") x✝   [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [Eq.symm](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___symm "Documentation for Eq.symm in Lean Language Reference")hy:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")x✝:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")h✝:x✝ [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") y⊢ x✝ [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") y   [assumption](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#assumption "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")All goals completed! 🐙 ```
After `[revert](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#revert "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") x`, the goal is:
y:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")⊢ ∀ (x : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")), x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") y → y [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") x
You can also revert multiple elements of the context at once:
`example (x y : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")) (h : x = y) : y = x := byx:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")y:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")h:x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") y⊢ y [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") x   [revert](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#revert "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") x y⊢ ∀ (x y : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")), x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") y → y [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") x   [intros](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intros "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")x✝:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")y✝:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")h✝:x✝ [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") y✝⊢ y✝ [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") x✝   [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [Eq.symm](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___symm "Documentation for Eq.symm in Lean Language Reference")hx✝:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")y✝:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")h✝:x✝ [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") y✝⊢ x✝ [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") y✝   [assumption](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#assumption "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")All goals completed! 🐙 ```
After `[revert](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#revert "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") x y`, the goal is:
⊢ ∀ (x y : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")), x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") y → y [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") x
You can only `[revert](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#revert "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` an element of the local context, that is, a local variable or hypothesis. But you can replace an arbitrary expression in the goal by a fresh variable using the `[generalize](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#generalize "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` tactic:
`example : 3 = 3 := by⊢ 3 [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") 3   [generalize](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#generalize "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") 3 = xx:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")⊢ x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") x   [revert](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#revert "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") x⊢ ∀ (x : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")), x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") x   [intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") yy:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")⊢ y [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") y   [rfl](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#rfl "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")All goals completed! 🐙 ```
In particular, after `[generalize](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#generalize "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")`, the goal is
x:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")⊢ x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") x
The mnemonic in the notation above is that you are generalizing the goal by setting `3` to an arbitrary variable `x`. Be careful: not every generalization preserves the validity of the goal. Here, `[generalize](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#generalize "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` replaces a goal that could be proved using `rfl` with one that is not provable:
``declaration uses 'sorry'`example : 2 + 3 = 5 := by⊢ 2 [+](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Type-Classes/Basic-Classes/#HAdd___mk "Documentation for HAdd.hAdd in Lean Language Reference") 3 [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") 5 [generalize](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#generalize "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") 3 = xx:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")⊢ 2 [+](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Type-Classes/Basic-Classes/#HAdd___mk "Documentation for HAdd.hAdd in Lean Language Reference") x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") 5 [sorry](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#sorry "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")All goals completed! 🐙 ```
In this example, the `[sorry](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#sorry "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` tactic is the analogue of the `sorry` proof term. It closes the current goal, producing the usual warning that `sorry` has been used. To preserve the validity of the previous goal, the `[generalize](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#generalize "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` tactic allows us to record the fact that `3` has been replaced by `x`. All you need to do is to provide a label, and `[generalize](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#generalize "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` uses it to store the assignment in the local context:
`example : 2 + 3 = 5 := by⊢ 2 [+](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Type-Classes/Basic-Classes/#HAdd___mk "Documentation for HAdd.hAdd in Lean Language Reference") 3 [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") 5   [generalize](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#generalize "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") h : 3 = xx:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")h:3 [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") x⊢ 2 [+](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Type-Classes/Basic-Classes/#HAdd___mk "Documentation for HAdd.hAdd in Lean Language Reference") x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") 5   [rw](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#rw "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [← h]All goals completed! 🐙 ```
Following `[generalize](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#generalize "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") h : 3 = x`, `h` is a proof that `3 = x`:
x:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")h:3 [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") x⊢ 2 [+](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Type-Classes/Basic-Classes/#HAdd___mk "Documentation for HAdd.hAdd in Lean Language Reference") x [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") 5
Here the rewriting tactic `[rw](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#rw "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` uses `h` to replace `x` by `3` again. The `[rw](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#rw "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` tactic will be discussed below.
##  5.3. More Tactics[🔗](find/?domain=Verso.Genre.Manual.section&name=more-tactics "Permalink")
Some additional tactics are useful for constructing and destructing propositions and data. For example, when applied to a goal of the form `p ∨ q`, you use tactics such as `[apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [Or.inl](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or.inl in Lean Language Reference")` and `[apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [Or.inr](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or.inr in Lean Language Reference")`. Conversely, the `[cases](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#cases "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` tactic can be used to decompose a disjunction:
`example (p q : Prop) : p ∨ q → q ∨ p := byp:Propq:Prop⊢ p [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") q → q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p   [intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hp:Propq:Proph:p [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") q⊢ q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p   [cases](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#cases "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") h with   | [inl](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or.inl in Lean Language Reference") hp =>inlp:Propq:Prophp:p⊢ q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [Or.inr](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or.inr in Lean Language Reference")inl.hp:Propq:Prophp:p⊢ p; [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hpAll goals completed! 🐙   | [inr](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or.inr in Lean Language Reference") hq =>inrp:Propq:Prophq:q⊢ q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [Or.inl](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or.inl in Lean Language Reference")inr.hp:Propq:Prophq:q⊢ q; [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hqAll goals completed! 🐙 ```
Note that the syntax is similar to the one used in `match` expressions. The new subgoals can be solved in any order:
`example (p q : Prop) : p ∨ q → q ∨ p := byp:Propq:Prop⊢ p [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") q → q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p   [intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hp:Propq:Proph:p [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") q⊢ q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p   [cases](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#cases "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") h with   | [inr](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or.inr in Lean Language Reference") hq =>inrp:Propq:Prophq:q⊢ q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [Or.inl](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or.inl in Lean Language Reference")inr.hp:Propq:Prophq:q⊢ q; [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hqAll goals completed! 🐙   | [inl](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or.inl in Lean Language Reference") hp =>inlp:Propq:Prophp:p⊢ q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [Or.inr](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or.inr in Lean Language Reference")inl.hp:Propq:Prophp:p⊢ p; [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hpAll goals completed! 🐙 ```
You can also use a (unstructured) `[cases](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#cases "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` without the `with` and a tactic for each alternative:
`example (p q : Prop) : p ∨ q → q ∨ p := byp:Propq:Prop⊢ p [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") q → q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p   [intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hp:Propq:Proph:p [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") q⊢ q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p   [cases](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#cases "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hinlp:Propq:Proph✝:p⊢ q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") pinrp:Propq:Proph✝:q⊢ q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p   [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [Or.inr](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or.inr in Lean Language Reference")inl.hp:Propq:Proph✝:p⊢ pinrp:Propq:Proph✝:q⊢ q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p   [assumption](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#assumption "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")inrp:Propq:Proph✝:q⊢ q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p   [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [Or.inl](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or.inl in Lean Language Reference")inr.hp:Propq:Proph✝:q⊢ q   [assumption](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#assumption "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")All goals completed! 🐙 ```
The (unstructured) `[cases](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#cases "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` is particularly useful when you can close several subgoals using the same tactic:
`example (p : Prop) : p ∨ p → p := byp:Prop⊢ p [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p → p   [intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hp:Proph:p [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p⊢ p   [cases](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#cases "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hinlp:Proph✝:p⊢ pinrp:Proph✝:p⊢ p   [repeat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#repeat "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [assumption](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#assumption "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")All goals completed! 🐙 ```
You can also use the combinator `tac1 ``<;>`` tac2` to apply `tac2` to each subgoal produced by tactic `tac1`:
`example (p : Prop) : p ∨ p → p := byp:Prop⊢ p [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p → p   [intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hp:Proph:p [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p⊢ p   [cases](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#cases "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hinlp:Proph✝:p⊢ pinrp:Proph✝:p⊢ p <;>inlp:Proph✝:p⊢ pinrp:Proph✝:p⊢ p [assumption](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#assumption "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")All goals completed! 🐙 ```
You can combine the unstructured `[cases](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#cases "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` tactic with the `[case](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/The-Tactic-Language/#case "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` and `.` notation:
`example (p q : Prop) : p ∨ q → q ∨ p := byp:Propq:Prop⊢ p [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") q → q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p   [intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hp:Propq:Proph:p [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") q⊢ q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p   [cases](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#cases "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hinlp:Propq:Proph✝:p⊢ q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") pinrp:Propq:Proph✝:q⊢ q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p   .inlp:Propq:Proph✝:p⊢ q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [Or.inr](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or.inr in Lean Language Reference")inl.hp:Propq:Proph✝:p⊢ p     [assumption](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#assumption "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")All goals completed! 🐙   .inrp:Propq:Proph✝:q⊢ q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [Or.inl](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or.inl in Lean Language Reference")inr.hp:Propq:Proph✝:q⊢ q     [assumption](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#assumption "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")All goals completed! 🐙  ``example (p q : Prop) : p ∨ q → q ∨ p := byp:Propq:Prop⊢ p [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") q → q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p   [intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hp:Propq:Proph:p [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") q⊢ q The `[cases](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#cases "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` tactic can also be used to decompose a conjunction:
`example (p q : Prop) : p ∧ q → q ∧ p := byp:Propq:Prop⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q → q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p   [intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hp:Propq:Proph:p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q⊢ q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p   [cases](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#cases "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") h with   | [intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference") hp hq =>introp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p [constructor](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#constructor "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")intro.leftp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ qintro.rightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p; [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hqintro.rightp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ p; [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hpAll goals completed! 🐙 ```
In this example, there is only one goal after the `[cases](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#cases "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` tactic is applied, with `h`` : ``p ∧ q` replaced by a pair of assumptions, `hp`` : ``p` and `hq`` : ``q`:
introp:Propq:Prophp:phq:q⊢ q [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p
The `[constructor](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#constructor "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` tactic applies the unique constructor for conjunction, `[And.intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference")`.
With these tactics, an example from the previous section can be rewritten as follows:
`example (p q r : Prop) : p ∧ (q ∨ r) ↔ (p ∧ q) ∨ (p ∧ r) := byp:Propq:Propr:Prop⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") [(](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference")q Reference") hrAll goals completed! 🐙 ```
You will see in [Inductive Types](Inductive-Types/#inductive-types) that these tactics are quite general. The `[cases](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#cases "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` tactic can be used to decompose any element of an inductively defined type; `[constructor](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#constructor "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` always applies the first applicable constructor of an inductively defined type. For example, you can use `[cases](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#cases "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` and `[constructor](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#constructor "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` with an existential quantifier:
`example (p q : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Prop) : (∃ x, p x) → ∃ x, p x ∨ q x := byp:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Propq:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Prop⊢ [(](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference")[∃](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") x[,](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") p x[)](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") → [∃](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") x[,](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") p x [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") q x   [intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hp:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Propq:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Proph:[∃](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") x[,](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") p x⊢ [∃](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") x[,](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") p x [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") q x   [cases](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#cases "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") h with   | [intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists.intro in Lean Language Reference") x px =>introp:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Propq:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Propx:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")px:p x⊢ [∃](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") x[,](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") p x [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") q x [constructor](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#constructor "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")intro.hp:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Propq:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Propx:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")px:p x⊢ p ?intro.w [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") q ?intro.wintro.wp:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Propq:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Propx:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")px:p x⊢ [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference"); [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [Or.inl](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or.inl in Lean Language Reference")intro.h.hp:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Propq:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Propx:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")px:p x⊢ p ?intro.wintro.wp:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Propq:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Propx:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")px:p x⊢ [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference"); [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") pxAll goals completed! 🐙 ```
Here, the `[constructor](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#constructor "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` tactic leaves the first component of the existential assertion, the value of `x`, implicit. It is represented by a metavariable, which should be instantiated later on. In the previous example, the proper value of the metavariable is determined by the tactic `[exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") px`, since `px` has type `p x`. If you want to specify a witness to the existential quantifier explicitly, you can use the `exists` tactic instead:
`example (p q : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Prop) : (∃ x, p x) → ∃ x, p x ∨ q x := byp:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Propq:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Prop⊢ [(](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference")[∃](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") x[,](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") p x[)](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") → [∃](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") x[,](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") p x [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") q x   [intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hp:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Propq:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Proph:[∃](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") x[,](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") p x⊢ [∃](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") x[,](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") p x [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") q x   [cases](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#cases "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") h with   | [intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists.intro in Lean Language Reference") x px =>introp:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Propq:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Propx:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")px:p x⊢ [∃](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") x[,](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") p x [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") q x [exists](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exists "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") xintrop:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") q x; Here is another example:
`example (p q : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Prop) : (∃ x, p x ∧ q x) → ∃ x, q x ∧ p x := byp:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → [(](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language x[,](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") p x [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q [∃](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p x =>introp:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q x⊢ [∃](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") x[,](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") q x [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p x     [cases](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#cases "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hpq with     | [intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.intro in Lean Language Reference") hp hq =>intro.introp:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Propq:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Propx:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")hp:p xhq:q x⊢ [∃](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") x[,](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Quantifiers/#Exists___intro "Documentation for Exists in Lean Language Reference") q x [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") p x       [exists](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exists "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") xAll goals completed! 🐙 ```
These tactics can be used on data just as well as propositions. In the next example, they are used to define functions which swap the components of the product and sum types:
`def swap_pair : α × β → β × α := byα:Type ?u.18β:Type ?u.17⊢ α [×](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Tuples/#Prod___mk "Documentation for Prod in Lean Language Reference") β → β [×](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Tuples/#Prod___mk "Documentation for Prod in Lean Language Reference") α   [intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") pα:Type ?u.18β:Type ?u.17p:α [×](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Tuples/#Prod___mk "Documentation for Prod in Lean Language Reference") β⊢ β [×](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Tuples/#Prod___mk "Documentation for Prod in Lean Language Reference") α   [cases](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#cases "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") pmkα:Type ?u.18β:Type ?u.17fst✝:αsnd✝:β⊢ β [×](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Tuples/#Prod___mk "Documentation for Prod in Lean Language Reference") α   [constructor](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#constructor "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")mk.fstα:Type ?u.18β:Type ?u.17fst✝:αsnd✝:β⊢ βmk.sndα:Type ?u.18β:Type ?u.17fst✝:αsnd✝:β⊢ α <;>mk.fstα:Type ?u.18β:Type ?u.17fst✝:αsnd✝:β⊢ βmk.sndα:Type ?u.18β:Type ?u.17fst✝:αsnd✝:β⊢ α [assumption](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#assumption "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")All goals completed! 🐙  ``def swap_sum : [Sum](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Sum-Types/#Sum___inl "Documentation for Sum in Lean Language Reference") α β → [⊕](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Sum-Types/#Sum___inl "Documentation for Sum in Lean Language Reference") β → β [assumption](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#assumption "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")All goals completed! 🐙 ```
Note that up to the names we have chosen for the variables, the definitions are identical to the proofs of the analogous propositions for conjunction and disjunction. The `[cases](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#cases "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` tactic will also do a case distinction on a natural number:
`[open](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Namespaces-and-Sections/#Lean___Parser___Command___open "Documentation for syntax in Lean Language Reference") Nat ``example (P : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference") → Prop)     (h₀ : P 0) (h₁ : ∀ n, P The `[cases](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#cases "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` tactic, and its companion, the `induction` tactic, are discussed in greater detail in the [Tactics for Inductive Types](Inductive-Types/#tactics-for-inductive-types) section.
The `[contradiction](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#contradiction "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` tactic searches for a contradiction among the hypotheses of the current goal:
`example (p q : Prop) : p ∧ ¬ p → q := byp:Propq:Prop⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") [¬](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Not "Documentation for Not in Lean Language Reference")p → q   [intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hp:Propq:Proph:p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") [¬](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Not "Documentation for Not in Lean Language Reference")p⊢ q   [cases](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#cases "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hintrop:Propq:Propleft✝:pright✝:[¬](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Not "Documentation for Not in Lean Language Reference")p⊢ q   [contradiction](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#contradiction "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")All goals completed! 🐙 ```
You can also use `match` in tactic blocks.
`example (p q r : Prop) : p ∧ (q ∨ r) ↔ (p ∧ q) ∨ (p ∧ r) := byp:Propq:Propr:Prop⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation ##  5.4. Structuring Tactic Proofs[🔗](find/?domain=Verso.Genre.Manual.section&name=structuring-tactic-proofs "Permalink")
Tactics often provide an efficient way of building a proof, but long sequences of instructions can obscure the structure of the argument. In this section, we describe some means that help provide structure to a tactic-style proof, making such proofs more readable and robust.
One thing that is nice about Lean's proof-writing syntax is that it is possible to mix term-style and tactic-style proofs, and pass between the two freely. For example, the tactics `[apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` and `[exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")` expect arbitrary terms, which you can write using `have`, `show`, and so on. Conversely, when writing an arbitrary Lean term, you can always invoke the tactic mode by inserting a `by` block. The following is a somewhat toy example:
`example (p q r : Prop) : p ∧ (q ∨ r) → (p ∧ q) ∨ (p ∧ r) := byp:Propq:Propr:Prop⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") [(](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference")q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") r[)](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") → p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") r   [intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") hp:Propq:Propr:Proph:p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") [(](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference")q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") r[)](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference")⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") r   [exact](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#exact "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")     have hp : p := h.[left](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.left in Lean Language Reference")     have hqr : q ∨ r := h.[right](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And.right in Lean Language Reference")     show (p ∧ q) ∨ (p ∧ r) byp:Propq:Propr:Prop⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") The following is a more natural example:

In fact, there is a `show` tactic, which is similar to the `show` expression in a proof term. It simply declares the type of the goal that is about to be solved, while remaining in tactic mode.
`example (p q r : Prop) : p ∧ (q ∨ r) ↔ (p ∧ q) ∨ (p ∧ r) := byp:Propq:Propr:Prop⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") [(](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference")q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") r[)](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") [↔](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Iff___intro "Documentation for Iff in Lean Language Reference") p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") r   [apply](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#apply "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [Iff.intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Iff___intro "Documentation for Iff.intro in Lean Language Reference")mpp:Propq:Propr:Prop⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") [(](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference")q The `show` tactic can actually be used to rewrite a goal to something definitionally equivalent:
`example (n : [Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")) : n + 1 = [Nat.succ](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat.succ in Lean Language Reference") n := byn:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")⊢ n [+](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Type-Classes/Basic-Classes/#HAdd___mk "Documentation for HAdd.hAdd in Lean Language Reference") 1 [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") n.[succ](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat.succ in Lean Language Reference")   [show](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#show "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") [Nat.succ](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat.succ in Lean Language Reference") n = [Nat.succ](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat.succ in Lean Language Reference") nn:[Nat](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat in Lean Language Reference")⊢ n.[succ](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat.succ in Lean Language Reference") [=](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Propositional-Equality/#Eq___refl "Documentation for Eq in Lean Language Reference") n.[succ](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Types/Natural-Numbers/#Nat___zero "Documentation for Nat.succ in Lean Language Reference")   [rfl](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#rfl "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference")All goals completed! 🐙 ```
There is also a `have` tactic, which introduces a new subgoal, just as when writing proof terms:
`example (p q r : Prop) : p ∧ (q ∨ r) → (p ∧ q) ∨ (p ∧ r) := byp:Propq:Propr:Prop⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") [(](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference")q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") r[)](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") → p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") r   [intro](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#intro "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") ⟨hp, hqr⟩p:Propq:Propr:Prophp:phqr:q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") r⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") r   [show](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Tactic-Proofs/Tactic-Reference/#show "Documentation for tactic in Lean Language Reference") (p ∧ q) ∨ (p ∧ r)p:Propq:Propr:Prophp:phqr:q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") r⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") r As with proof terms, you can omit the label in the `have` tactic, in which case, the default label `this` is used:
`example (p q r : Prop) : p ∧ (q ∨ r) → (p ∧ q) ∨ (p ∧ r) := byp:Propq:Propr:Prop⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation The types in a `have` tactic can be omitted, so you can write `have hp := h.left` and `have hqr := h.right`. In fact, with this notation, you can even omit both the type and the label, in which case the new fact is introduced with the label `this`:
`example (p q r : Prop) : p ∧ (q ∨ r) → (p ∧ q) ∨ (p ∧ r) := byp:Propq:Propr:Prop⊢ p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") [(](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference")q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") r[)](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") → p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") r [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") q [∨](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#Or___inl "Documentation for Or in Lean Language Reference") p [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") r [∧](https://lean-lang.org/doc/reference/4.26.0/Basic-Propositions/Logical-Connectives/#And___intro "Documentation for And in Lean Language Reference") r
